Clinton Presidential Center and Park</a> in <a href="/wiki/Little_Rock,_Arkansas" title="Little Rock, Arkansas">Little Rock, Arkansas</a> was dedicated in 2004.<sup id="cite_ref-219" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-219"><span>[</span>219<span>]</span></a></sup> Clinton released a best-selling autobiography, <i><a href="/wiki/My_Life_(Bill_Clinton_autobiography)" title="My Life (Bill Clinton autobiography)">My Life</a></i> in 2004.<sup id="cite_ref-220" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-220"><span>[</span>220<span>]</span></a></sup> In 2007, he released <i><a href="/wiki/Giving:_How_Each_of_Us_Can_Change_the_World" title="Giving: How Each of Us Can Change the World">Giving: How Each of Us Can Change the World</a></i>, which also became a <a href="/wiki/The_New_York_Times_Best_Seller_list" title="The New York Times Best Seller list"><i>The New York Times</i> Best Seller</a> and garnered positive reviews.<sup id="cite_ref-221" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-221"><span>[</span>221<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Bush_and_Clinton.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cc/Bush_and_Clinton.jpg/220px-Bush_and_Clinton.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cc/Bush_and_Clinton.jpg/330px-Bush_and_Clinton.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cc/Bush_and_Clinton.jpg/440px-Bush_and_Clinton.jpg 2x" data-file-width="515" data-file-height="343" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Bush_and_Clinton.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Clinton with former President George H. W. Bush in January 2005</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>In the aftermath of the <a href="/wiki/2004_Indian_Ocean_earthquake_and_tsunami" title="2004 Indian Ocean earthquake and tsunami">2004 Asian tsunami</a>, <a href="/wiki/Secretary-General_of_the_United_Nations" title="Secretary-General of the United Nations">U.N. Secretary-General</a> <a href="/wiki/Kofi_Annan" title="Kofi Annan">Kofi Annan</a> appointed Clinton to head a relief effort.<sup id="cite_ref-222" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-222"><span>[</span>222<span>]</span></a></sup> After <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Katrina" title="Hurricane Katrina">Hurricane Katrina</a>, Clinton joined with fellow former President George H. W. Bush to establish the Bush-Clinton Tsunami Fund in January 2005, and the Bush-Clinton Katrina Fund in October of that year.<sup id="cite_ref-223" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-223"><span>[</span>223<span>]</span></a></sup> As part of the tsunami effort, these two ex-presidents appeared in a <a href="/wiki/Super_Bowl_XXXIX" title="Super Bowl XXXIX">Super Bowl XXXIX</a> pre-game show,<sup id="cite_ref-224" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-224"><span>[</span>224<span>]</span></a></sup> and traveled to the affected areas.<sup id="cite_ref-225" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-225"><span>[</span>225<span>]</span></a></sup> They also spoke together at the funeral of <a href="/wiki/Boris_Yeltsin" title="Boris Yeltsin">Boris Yeltsin</a> in 2007.<sup id="cite_ref-226" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-226"><span>[</span>226<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Clinton_pres_library.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Clinton_pres_library.jpg/220px-Clinton_pres_library.jpg" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Clinton_pres_library.jpg/330px-Clinton_pres_library.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Clinton_pres_library.jpg/440px-Clinton_pres_library.jpg 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="450" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Clinton_pres_library.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/William_J._Clinton_Presidential_Center_and_Park" title="William J. Clinton Presidential Center and Park" class="mw-redirect">William J. Clinton Presidential Center and Park</a>, dedicated in 2004</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Based on his philanthropic worldview,<sup id="cite_ref-227" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-227"><span>[</span>227<span>]</span></a></sup> Clinton created the <a href="/wiki/William_J._Clinton_Foundation" title="William J. Clinton Foundation" class="mw-redirect">William J. Clinton Foundation</a> to address issues of global importance. This foundation includes the Clinton Foundation HIV and AIDS Initiative (CHAI), which strives to combat that disease, and has worked with the Australian government toward that end. The Clinton Global Initiative (CGI), begun by the Clinton Foundation in 2005, attempts to address world problems such as global <a href="/wiki/Public_health" title="Public health">public health</a>, poverty alleviation and religious and <a href="/wiki/Ethnic_conflict" title="Ethnic conflict">ethnic conflict</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-228" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-228"><span>[</span>228<span>]</span></a></sup> In 2005, Clinton announced through his foundation an agreement with manufacturers to stop selling sugared drinks in schools.<sup id="cite_ref-229" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-229"><span>[</span>229<span>]</span></a></sup> Clinton's foundation joined with the <a href="/wiki/Large_Cities_Climate_Leadership_Group" title="Large Cities Climate Leadership Group" class="mw-redirect">Large Cities Climate Leadership Group</a> in 2006 to improve cooperation among those cities, and he met with foreign leaders to promote this initiative.<sup id="cite_ref-230" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-230"><span>[</span>230<span>]</span></a></sup> The foundation has received donations from a number of governments all over the world, including Asia and the Middle East.<sup id="cite_ref-theage.com.au_231-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-theage.com.au-231"><span>[</span>231<span>]</span></a></sup> In 2008, Foundation director <a href="/wiki/Inder_Singh_(philanthropist)" title="Inder Singh (philanthropist)">Inder Singh</a> announced deals to reduce the price of anti-malaria drugs by 30&#160;percent in developing nations.<sup id="cite_ref-232" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-232"><span>[</span>232<span>]</span></a></sup> Clinton also spoke in favor of <a href="/wiki/California_Proposition_87_(2006)" title="California Proposition 87 (2006)">California Proposition 87</a> on <a href="/wiki/Energy_development" title="Energy development">alternative energy</a>, which was voted down.<sup id="cite_ref-233" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-233"><span>[</span>233<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Presidential_election_2008">Presidential election 2008</span></h3>
<p>During the <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_presidential_primaries,_2008" title="Democratic Party presidential primaries, 2008">2008 Democratic presidential primary campaign</a>, Clinton vigorously advocated on behalf of his wife, <a href="/wiki/Hillary_Clinton" title="Hillary Clinton">Hillary Clinton</a>. Through speaking engagements and fundraisers, he was able to raise $10&#160;million toward her campaign.<sup id="cite_ref-234" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-234"><span>[</span>234<span>]</span></a></sup> Some worried that as an ex-president, he was too active on the trail, too negative to Clinton rival Barack Obama, and alienating his supporters at home and abroad.<sup id="cite_ref-CBS-Tarnish_235-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CBS-Tarnish-235"><span>[</span>235<span>]</span></a></sup> Many were especially critical of him following his remarks in the South Carolina primary, which Obama won. Later in the 2008 primaries, there was some infighting between Bill and Hillary's staffs, especially in Pennsylvania.<sup id="cite_ref-autogenerated3_236-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autogenerated3-236"><span>[</span>236<span>]</span></a></sup> Considering Bill's remarks, many thought that he could not rally Hillary supporters behind Obama after Obama won the primary.<sup id="cite_ref-237" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-237"><span>[</span>237<span>]</span></a></sup> Such remarks lead to apprehension that the party would be split to the detriment of Obama's election. Fears were allayed August 27, 2008, when Clinton enthusiastically endorsed Obama at the <a href="/wiki/2008_Democratic_National_Convention" title="2008 Democratic National Convention">2008 Democratic National Convention</a>, saying that all his experience as president assures him that Obama is "ready to lead."<sup id="cite_ref-238" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-238"><span>[</span>238<span>]</span></a></sup> After Hillary Clinton's presidential campaign was over, Bill Clinton continued to raise funds to help pay off her campaign debt.<sup id="cite_ref-239" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-239"><span>[</span>239<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-240" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-240"><span>[</span>240<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="After_the_2008_election">After the 2008 election</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Obama_and_Bill_Clinton.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b8/Obama_and_Bill_Clinton.jpg/220px-Obama_and_Bill_Clinton.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b8/Obama_and_Bill_Clinton.jpg/330px-Obama_and_Bill_Clinton.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b8/Obama_and_Bill_Clinton.jpg/440px-Obama_and_Bill_Clinton.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4096" data-file-height="2731" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Obama_and_Bill_Clinton.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Clinton with President Barack Obama and Senior Advisor <a href="/wiki/Valerie_Jarrett" title="Valerie Jarrett">Valerie Jarrett</a> in July 2010</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>In 2009, Clinton travelled to <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> on behalf of <a href="/wiki/2009_imprisonment_of_American_journalists_by_North_Korea" title="2009 imprisonment of American journalists by North Korea">two American journalists imprisoned in North Korea</a>. <a href="/wiki/Euna_Lee" title="Euna Lee">Euna Lee</a> and <a href="/wiki/Laura_Ling" title="Laura Ling">Laura Ling</a> had been imprisoned for illegally entering the country from China.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCDPRK_241-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCDPRK-241"><span>[</span>241<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Jimmy_Carter" title="Jimmy Carter">Jimmy Carter</a> had made a similar visit in 1994.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCDPRK_241-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCDPRK-241"><span>[</span>241<span>]</span></a></sup> After Clinton met with North Korean leader <a href="/wiki/Kim_Jong-il" title="Kim Jong-il">Kim Jong-il</a>, Kim issued a pardon.<sup id="cite_ref-242" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-242"><span>[</span>242<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-243" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-243"><span>[</span>243<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>Since then, Clinton has been assigned a number of other diplomatic missions. He was named United Nations <a href="/wiki/Special_Envoy_of_the_Secretary-General" title="Special Envoy of the Secretary-General">Special Envoy</a> to <a href="/wiki/Haiti" title="Haiti">Haiti</a> in 2009.<sup id="cite_ref-haiti_244-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-haiti-244"><span>[</span>244<span>]</span></a></sup> In response to the <a href="/wiki/2010_Haiti_earthquake" title="2010 Haiti earthquake">2010 Haiti earthquake</a>, U.S. President Barack Obama announced that Clinton and <a href="/wiki/George_W._Bush" title="George W. Bush">George W. Bush</a> would coordinate efforts to raise funds for Haiti's recovery.<sup id="cite_ref-245" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-245"><span>[</span>245<span>]</span></a></sup> Clinton continues to visit Haiti to witness the inauguration of refugee villages, and to raise funds for victims of the earthquake.<sup id="cite_ref-246" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-246"><span>[</span>246<span>]</span></a></sup> In 2010, Clinton announced support of, and delivered the keynote address for, the inauguration of <a href="/wiki/NTR_Foundation" title="NTR Foundation" class="mw-redirect">NTR</a>, Ireland's first environmental foundation.<sup id="cite_ref-247" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-247"><span>[</span>247<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-248" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-248"><span>[</span>248<span>]</span></a></sup> At the <a href="/wiki/2012_Democratic_National_Convention" title="2012 Democratic National Convention">2012 Democratic National Convention</a>, Clinton gave a widely praised speech nominating Barack Obama.<sup id="cite_ref-249" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-249"><span>[</span>249<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-presidential_health_concerns">Post-presidential health concerns</span></h3>
<p>In September 2004, Clinton received a quadruple bypass surgery.<sup id="cite_ref-news.bbc.co.uk_250-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-news.bbc.co.uk-250"><span>[</span>250<span>]</span></a></sup> In March 2005, he underwent surgery for a partially collapsed lung.<sup id="cite_ref-251" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-251"><span>[</span>251<span>]</span></a></sup> On February 11, 2010, he was rushed to <a href="/wiki/Columbia_Presbyterian_Hospital" title="Columbia Presbyterian Hospital" class="mw-redirect">Columbia Presbyterian Hospital</a> in New York City after complaining of chest pains, and had two <a href="/wiki/Coronary_stent" title="Coronary stent">coronary stents</a> implanted in his heart.<sup id="cite_ref-news.bbc.co.uk_250-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-news.bbc.co.uk-250"><span>[</span>250<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-252" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-252"><span>[</span>252<span>]</span></a></sup> After this experience, Clinton adopted the plant-based whole foods (<a href="/wiki/Veganism" title="Veganism">vegan</a>) diet recommended by doctors <a href="/wiki/Dean_Ornish" title="Dean Ornish">Dean Ornish</a> and <a href="/wiki/Caldwell_Esselstyn" title="Caldwell Esselstyn">Caldwell Esselstyn</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-cnn2011_253-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cnn2011-253"><span>[</span>253<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>Clinton has reportedly begun practicing <a href="/wiki/Buddhist_meditation" title="Buddhist meditation">Buddhist meditation</a> in order to help him relax.<sup id="cite_ref-http:.2F.2Fwww.dailymail.co.uk.2Fnews.2Farticle-2183101.2FBill-Clinton-turns-art-Buddhist-meditation-relax.html_254-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-http:.2F.2Fwww.dailymail.co.uk.2Fnews.2Farticle-2183101.2FBill-Clinton-turns-art-Buddhist-meditation-relax.html-254"><span>[</span>254<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Income_and_personal_finances">Income and personal finances</span></h3>
<p>The Clintons accrued several million dollars in legal bills during his presidency; they were paid off four years after he left office.<sup id="cite_ref-255" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-255"><span>[</span>255<span>]</span></a></sup> Both Bill and Hillary Clinton have received millions of dollars in book authorship fees.<sup id="cite_ref-NYT-2008-04-05_256-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NYT-2008-04-05-256"><span>[</span>256<span>]</span></a></sup> In May 2015, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Hill_(newspaper)" title="The Hill (newspaper)">The Hill</a></i> reported that Bill and Hillary Clinton have made more than $25 million in speaking fees since the start of 2014, and that Hillary Clinton also made $5 million or more from her book, <i><a href="/wiki/Hard_Choices" title="Hard Choices">Hard Choices</a>,</i> during the same time period.<sup id="cite_ref-257" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-257"><span>[</span>257<span>]</span></a></sup> In July 2014, the <i><a href="/wiki/Mail_Online" title="Mail Online">Daily Mail</a></i> reported that together, the couple "has earned more than $160 million in the decade after Bill's second presidential term came to an end."<sup id="cite_ref-258" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-258"><span>[</span>258<span>]</span></a></sup> Also in July 2014, the <i><a href="/wiki/Wall_Street_Journal" title="Wall Street Journal" class="mw-redirect">Wall Street Journal</a></i> reported that at the end of 2012, the Clintons were worth between $5 million and $25.5 million, and that in 2012 (the last year they were required to disclose the information) the Clintons made between $16 and $17 million, mostly from speaking fees earned by the former president.<sup id="cite_ref-259" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-259"><span>[</span>259<span>]</span></a></sup> Clinton earned more than $104 million from paid speeches between 2001 and 2012.<sup id="cite_ref-bloomberg.com_260-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bloomberg.com-260"><span>[</span>260<span>]</span></a></sup> In June 2014, <i>ABC News</i> and <i>The Washington Post</i> reported that Bill Clinton has made more than $100 million giving paid speeches since leaving public office, and in 2008, the <i>New York Times</i> reported that the Clintons' income tax returns<sup id="cite_ref-261" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-261"><span>[</span>261<span>]</span></a></sup> show they have made $109 million in the 8 years from January 1, 2000 to December 31, 2007, including almost $92 million from his speaking and book-writing.<sup id="cite_ref-NYT-2008-04-05_256-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NYT-2008-04-05-256"><span>[</span>256<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-washingtonpost-2014-06-26_262-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-washingtonpost-2014-06-26-262"><span>[</span>262<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ABC-News-2014-06-09_263-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ABC-News-2014-06-09-263"><span>[</span>263<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-264" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-264"><span>[</span>264<span>]</span></a></sup> Hillary Clinton said that she and Bill came out of the White House financially "broke" and in debt, especially due to large legal fees incurred during their years in the White House. "We had no money when we got there, and we struggled to, you know, piece together the resources for mortgages, for houses, for Chelsea's education." She added, "Bill has worked really hard…we had to pay off all our debts…he had to make double the money because of, obviously, taxes; and then pay off the debts, and get us houses, and take care of family members."<sup id="cite_ref-ABC-News-2014-06-09_263-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ABC-News-2014-06-09-263"><span>[</span>263<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>Clinton has given dozens of paid speeches each year, mostly to corporations and philanthropic groups in North America and Europe, often earning $100,000 to $300,000 per speech.<sup id="cite_ref-265" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-265"><span>[</span>265<span>]</span></a></sup> According to his wife's Senate ethics reports, he earned more than $30 million in speaking from 2001 to 2005.<sup id="cite_ref-266" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-266"><span>[</span>266<span>]</span></a></sup> In 2007, it is estimated he amassed around $40 million from speaking.<sup id="cite_ref-267" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-267"><span>[</span>267<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Honors_and_recognition">Honors and recognition</span></h2>
<div class="hatnote relarticle mainarticle">Main article: <a href="/wiki/List_of_honors_and_awards_earned_by_Bill_Clinton" title="List of honors and awards earned by Bill Clinton" class="mw-redirect">List of honors and awards earned by Bill Clinton</a></div>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:William_S._Cohen_presents_President_Clinton_the_Department_of_Defense_Medal_for_Distinguished_Public_Service.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6e/William_S._Cohen_presents_President_Clinton_the_Department_of_Defense_Medal_for_Distinguished_Public_Service.jpg/220px-William_S._Cohen_presents_President_Clinton_the_Department_of_Defense_Medal_for_Distinguished_Public_Service.jpg" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6e/William_S._Cohen_presents_President_Clinton_the_Department_of_Defense_Medal_for_Distinguished_Public_Service.jpg/330px-William_S._Cohen_presents_President_Clinton_the_Department_of_Defense_Medal_for_Distinguished_Public_Service.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6e/William_S._Cohen_presents_President_Clinton_the_Department_of_Defense_Medal_for_Distinguished_Public_Service.jpg/440px-William_S._Cohen_presents_President_Clinton_the_Department_of_Defense_Medal_for_Distinguished_Public_Service.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2907" data-file-height="1929" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">

<a href="/wiki/United_States_Secretary_of_Defense" title="United States Secretary of Defense">Secretary of Defense</a> <a href="/wiki/William_Cohen" title="William Cohen">Cohen</a> presents President Clinton the DoD Medal for Distinguished Public Service.</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Bill_Clinton_statue.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/Bill_Clinton_statue.jpg/220px-Bill_Clinton_statue.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/Bill_Clinton_statue.jpg/330px-Bill_Clinton_statue.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/Bill_Clinton_statue.jpg/440px-Bill_Clinton_statue.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3872" data-file-height="2592" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Bill_Clinton_statue.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Bill Clinton statue in <a href="/wiki/Pristina" title="Pristina">Pristina</a>, the capital of the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Kosovo" title="Republic of Kosovo" class="mw-redirect">Republic of Kosovo</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Various colleges and universities have awarded Clinton <a href="/wiki/Honorary_degrees" title="Honorary degrees" class="mw-redirect">honorary degrees</a>, including <a href="/wiki/Legum_Doctor" title="Legum Doctor">Doctorate of Law</a> degrees<sup id="cite_ref-268" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-268"><span>[</span>268<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-269" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-269"><span>[</span>269<span>]</span></a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Doctor_of_Humane_Letters" title="Doctor of Humane Letters">Doctor of Humane Letters</a> degrees.<sup id="cite_ref-270" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-270"><span>[</span>270<span>]</span></a></sup> He is an Honorary Fellow of University College, Oxford, which he attended as a <a href="/wiki/Rhodes_Scholar" title="Rhodes Scholar" class="mw-redirect">Rhodes Scholar</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-271" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-271"><span>[</span>271<span>]</span></a></sup> Schools have been named for Clinton,<sup id="cite_ref-272" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-272"><span>[</span>272<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-273" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-273"><span>[</span>273<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-274" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-274"><span>[</span>274<span>]</span></a></sup> and statues have been built to pay him homage.<sup id="cite_ref-WJCstatue_275-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WJCstatue-275"><span>[</span>275<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-276" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-276"><span>[</span>276<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-277" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-277"><span>[</span>277<span>]</span></a></sup> U.S. states where he has been honored include Missouri,<sup id="cite_ref-DeMolay-1_278-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DeMolay-1-278"><span>[</span>278<span>]</span></a></sup> Arkansas,<sup id="cite_ref-279" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-279"><span>[</span>279<span>]</span></a></sup> Kentucky,<sup id="cite_ref-HOOKC_280-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HOOKC-280"><span>[</span>280<span>]</span></a></sup> and New York.<sup id="cite_ref-281" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-281"><span>[</span>281<span>]</span></a></sup> He was presented with the <a href="/wiki/Medal_for_Distinguished_Public_Service" title="Medal for Distinguished Public Service" class="mw-redirect">Medal for Distinguished Public Service</a> by <a href="/wiki/United_States_Secretary_of_Defense" title="United States Secretary of Defense">Secretary of Defense</a> <a href="/wiki/William_S._Cohen" title="William S. Cohen" class="mw-redirect">William S. Cohen</a> in 2001.<sup id="cite_ref-282" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-282"><span>[</span>282<span>]</span></a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Clinton_Presidential_Center" title="Clinton Presidential Center">Clinton Presidential Center</a> was opened in <a href="/wiki/Little_Rock,_Arkansas" title="Little Rock, Arkansas">Little Rock, Arkansas</a> in his honor on December 5, 2001.<sup id="cite_ref-NYT_283-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NYT-283"><span>[</span>283<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>He has been honored in various other ways, in countries that include the Czech Republic,<sup id="cite_ref-284" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-284"><span>[</span>284<span>]</span></a></sup> Papua New Guinea,<sup id="cite_ref-285" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-285"><span>[</span>285<span>]</span></a></sup> Germany,<sup id="cite_ref-286" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-286"><span>[</span>286<span>]</span></a></sup> and Kosovo.<sup id="cite_ref-WJCstatue_275-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WJCstatue-275"><span>[</span>275<span>]</span></a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Kosovo" title="Republic of Kosovo" class="mw-redirect">Republic of Kosovo</a>, in gratitude for his help during the <a href="/wiki/Kosovo_War" title="Kosovo War">Kosovo War</a>, renamed a major street in the capital city of <a href="/wiki/Pristina" title="Pristina">Pristina</a> as <a href="/wiki/Bill_Clinton_Boulevard" title="Bill Clinton Boulevard">Bill Clinton Boulevard</a> and added a monumental Clinton statue.<sup id="cite_ref-287" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-287"><span>[</span>287<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-288" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-288"><span>[</span>288<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-289" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-289"><span>[</span>289<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>Clinton was selected as <i><a href="/wiki/Time_(magazine)" title="Time (magazine)">Time</a></i>???'??s "<a href="/wiki/Time_Person_of_the_Year" title="Time Person of the Year">Man of the Year</a>" in 1992,<sup id="cite_ref-290" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-290"><span>[</span>290<span>]</span></a></sup> and again in 1998, along with <a href="/wiki/Ken_Starr" title="Ken Starr">Ken Starr</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-291" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-291"><span>[</span>291<span>]</span></a></sup> From a poll conducted of the American people in December 1999, Clinton was among eighteen included in <a href="/wiki/Gallup%27s_List_of_Widely_Admired_People" title="Gallup's List of Widely Admired People" class="mw-redirect">Gallup's List of Widely Admired People</a> of the 20th century.<sup id="cite_ref-292" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-292"><span>[</span>292<span>]</span></a></sup> He was honored with a <a href="/wiki/Grammy_Award_for_Best_Spoken_Word_Album_for_Children" title="Grammy Award for Best Spoken Word Album for Children">Grammy Award for Best Spoken Word Album for Children</a>, a <a href="/wiki/J._William_Fulbright" title="J. William Fulbright">J. William Fulbright</a> Prize for International Understanding,<sup id="cite_ref-293" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-293"><span>[</span>293<span>]</span></a></sup> a <a href="/wiki/TED_(conference)" title="TED (conference)">TED</a> Prize (named for the confluence of technology, entertainment and design),<sup id="cite_ref-294" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-294"><span>[</span>294<span>]</span></a></sup> and was named as an Honorary <a href="/wiki/GLAAD_Media_Award" title="GLAAD Media Award">GLAAD Media Award</a> recipient for his work as an advocate for the <a href="/wiki/LGBT" title="LGBT">LGBT</a> community.<sup id="cite_ref-24-GLAAD-LA_295-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24-GLAAD-LA-295"><span>[</span>295<span>]</span></a></sup> U.S. President Barack Obama awarded Clinton the <a href="/wiki/Presidential_Medal_of_Freedom" title="Presidential Medal of Freedom">Presidential Medal of Freedom</a> on November 20, 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-Medal_of_Honor_296-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Medal_of_Honor-296"><span>[</span>296<span>]</span></a></sup></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Recordings">Recordings</span></h2>
<p>Bill Clinton is one of the narrators on a 2003 recording of <a href="/wiki/Sergei_Prokofiev" title="Sergei Prokofiev">Sergei Prokofiev</a>'s <i>Peter and the Wolf</i>, on <a href="/wiki/PentaTone_Classics" title="PentaTone Classics" class="mw-redirect">Pentatone</a>, together with <a href="/wiki/Mikhail_Gorbachev" title="Mikhail Gorbachev">Mikhail Gorbachev</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sophia_Loren" title="Sophia Loren">Sophia Loren</a>.</p>

(= a member of the <a href="/wiki/Southern_Baptist_Convention" title="Southern Baptist Convention">Southern Baptist Convention</a> SBC). Washington, D.C.: Regnery Publishing, 1998. 275 p. + [8] p. of col. photos. <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0895263335" class="internal mw-magiclink-isbn">ISBN 0-89526-333-5</a></li>

<div style="font-size:114%"><a href="/wiki/Grammy_Award_for_Best_Spoken_Word_Album" title="Grammy Award for Best Spoken Word Album">Grammy Award for Best Spoken Word Album</a> (2000s)</div>

<td colspan="2" class="navbox-list navbox-odd hlist" style="width:100%;padding:0px">
<div style="padding:0em 0.25em">
<dl>
<dt>2000</dt>
<dd><a href="/wiki/LeVar_Burton" title="LeVar Burton">LeVar Burton</a> - <i>The Autobiography of <a href="/wiki/Martin_Luther_King,_Jr." title="Martin Luther King, Jr.">Martin Luther King, Jr.</a></i></dd>
<dt>2001</dt>
<dd><a href="/wiki/Sidney_Poitier" title="Sidney Poitier">Sidney Poitier</a>, Rick Harris, John Runnette (producers) - <i><a href="/wiki/The_Measure_of_a_Man:_A_Spiritual_Autobiography" title="The Measure of a Man: A Spiritual Autobiography">The Measure of a Man: A Spiritual Autobiography</a></i></dd>
<dt>2002</dt>
<dd><a href="/wiki/Quincy_Jones" title="Quincy Jones">Quincy Jones</a>, Jeffrey S. Thomas, Steven Strassman (engineers), Elisa Shokoff]] (producer) - <i>Q: The Autobiography of Quincy Jones</i></dd>
<dt>2003</dt>
<dd><a href="/wiki/Maya_Angelou" title="Maya Angelou">Maya Angelou</a>, Charles B. Potter (producer) - <i><a href="/wiki/A_Song_Flung_Up_to_Heaven" title="A Song Flung Up to Heaven">A Song Flung Up to Heaven</a></i> / <a href="/wiki/Robin_Williams" title="Robin Williams">Robin Williams</a>, Nathaniel Kunkel (engineer/mixer), <a href="/wiki/Peter_Asher" title="Peter Asher">Peter Asher</a> (producer) - <i><a href="/wiki/Robin_Williams:_Live_on_Broadway" title="Robin Williams: Live on Broadway" class="mw-redirect">Live 2002</a></i></dd>
<dt>2004</dt>
<dd><a href="/wiki/Al_Franken" title="Al Franken">Al Franken</a>, <a href="/w/index.php?title=Paul_Ruben&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Paul Ruben (page does not exist)">Paul Ruben</a> (producer)- <i><a href="/wiki/Lies_and_the_Lying_Liars_Who_Tell_Them" title="Lies and the Lying Liars Who Tell Them">Lies and the Lying Liars Who Tell Them</a></i></dd>
<dt>2005</dt>
<dd><strong class="selflink">Bill Clinton</strong> - <i><a href="/wiki/My_Life_(Bill_Clinton_autobiography)" title="My Life (Bill Clinton autobiography)">My Life</a></i></dd>
<dt>2006</dt>
<dd><a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> - <i><a href="/wiki/Dreams_from_My_Father" title="Dreams from My Father">Dreams from My Father</a></i></dd>
<dt>2007</dt>
<dd><a href="/wiki/Jimmy_Carter" title="Jimmy Carter">Jimmy Carter</a> - <i><a href="/wiki/Our_Endangered_Values" title="Our Endangered Values">Our Endangered Values: America's Moral Crisis</a></i> / <a href="/wiki/Ossie_Davis" title="Ossie Davis">Ossie Davis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ruby_Dee" title="Ruby Dee">Ruby Dee</a> - <i>With Ossie and Ruby</i></dd>
<dt>2008</dt>
